discoveri iceland norwegian ninth century

It foreign present object attempt delin
pirat even frequent conquer expedit variou
nation scandinavia name angl saxon jute
dane norman long harass fragment roman empir
about year one naddod nordman norwegian vikingr chief
band freeboot voyag faro island thrown
storm upon eastern coast unknown countri consider
beyond ordinari cours navig gave signific
name snioland snowland immens quantiti snow
everi cover numer lofti mountain even height
summer fill mani valley long dreari winter As
naddod gave rather favour account discoveri return
norway one gardar suafarson swedish origin settl norway
determin upon make expedit snowland
circumnavig whole extent new discoveri name
gardarsholm gardarsisland

gardar employ long time expedit deem
safe navig northern ocean storm winter
remain island ensu spring sail norway
He report though island entir cover wood
respect fine countri from favour natur
report one flock son vigvardar acquir great
reput among nordmen norman experienc intrepid
vikingr pirat resolv visit newlydiscov island flock
likewis winter northern part island met
immens quantiti drift ice circumst chose give
name iceland still bear He mean pleas
countri influenc doubt unfavour impress
imbib spend long protract winter dreari northern
shore amid almost everdur arctic ice surround
unpromis steril though companion repres
land pleas fertil desir visit iceland seem
time lain dormant among adventur norwegian navig
probabl neither fame rich could acquir either
traffic depred countri utterli destitut
inhabit

At length two friend ingolf lief repair iceland
much satisfi appear form resolut
attempt make settlement countri induc doubtless
desir withdraw continu war revolut
harass north europ escap thraldom
incipi monarchi norway denmark sweden impos
upon independ chief vikingr norman In pursuanc
determin ingolf transport peopl iceland year
sever cattl kind implement enabl
commenc coloni At period friend lief absent english
war went soon afterward iceland carri booti
acquir england

bell crozier coast whenc imagin
peopl ireland resid previou discoveri

articl might wash shore Or may attribut

voyag ohther white sea baltic ninth
century

some norwegian chieftain dissatisfi usurp
suprem author harold took refug england alfr
recent settl mani vanquish dane nordmen northern
part dominion almost entir depopul laid
wast longcontinu destruct ravag among one
ohther made famou voyag unknown part
north invit court alfr give account
discoveri observ made unusu expedit
thi person chief note countri dwelt
place call halgoland suppos
numadalen other say nordland northerli p provinc
norway proper In succeed paragraph said dwelt
opposit west sea  alfr use word sea
denot confin expans narrow channel call ocean
garsecg seem highli probabl west sea west
ford intend channel strait divid luffoden
island coast nordland would clearli place resid
ohther northern provinc the account gave
voyag royal patron follow

ohther told lord king alfr lie live north
nordmen norwegian dwelt land northward
opposit west sea land north sea
wast uninhabit except place finan
fin repair winter hunt fowl fish
summer be desir ascertain far countri extend toward
north whether inhabit beyond wast
proceed sea due north habit leav desert land
way starboard righthand wide sea
larboard lefthand cours after three day sail far
north whalehunt ever go proceed cours due
north three day found land instead stretch
due north hitherto trend thenc toward east whether
sea lie within land knew wait
west wind sail near land eastward far could
four day found direct coast chang due
south wait north wind sail due south far
could five day

In land found larg river mouth lay
could proceed much farther account inhabit
hostil all land one side river inhabit
toler well cultiv met inhabit till
sinc left countri whole land right
desert without inhabit except fisher fowler hunter
beforement fin open sea lay left hand
whole voyag the beorma inde well peopl
countri reason ventur enter upon land
terfenna pass hitherto desert
except hunter fisher alreadi mention

the beorma told mani particular land
neighbour countri could reli account
opportun see eye seem
beorma fin spoke languag ohther state
motiv expedit besid littl curios explor
countri unknown countrymen princip pursuit
horsewhal valuabl tusk excel
ivori brought king hide serv
make rope ship thi speci whale much smaller
kind seldom seven ell length
speci often fortyeight ell long sometim even fifti In
countri best whalefish ohther ever seen
whale numer one six kill threescor
three day

ohther rich man thing consid
valuabl countri possess time came
king six hundr tame deer none bought besid
six decoy deer much request among fin mean
enabl catch wild deer yet though one
richest men part twenti head cattl twenti

two cabl ship rope sixti ell long one made
whale hide skin seal

accord descript given king ohther northmannaland
norway long narrow land fit pastur
tillag seacoast rocki place To
east parallel cultiv land wild
huge mountain moor inhabit fin the cultiv

place middl countri perhap thirti
mile broad somewhat narrowest north
hardli three mile sea moor In place

opposit south part countri sueoland sweden

halgoland sciringesh As proce northward great

of monstrou men like dog conquest burithabeth

shape male shape great dog after time
